  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_237a57b4-ba5a-410b-a0f2-3faf88ac4613'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };
    if (typeof AppleID !== "undefined") {
      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();
    }

She’s been marked as Satan’s bride and her jealous fiancé wants her all to himself. The only way this Horseman can keep herself—and everyone else—safe is to keep her distance. But not even Limos can save herself from the secrets she’s kept . . . or resist the seductive allure of one very brave human.<br /><br />Arik Wagner knows the saying “love hurts” better than most, yet he never thought stealing a kiss from Limos would land him in Hell. Literally. It takes all his military training to survive the demon torture, but once he’s topside, Arik realizes that the agony has just begun. With the Apocalypse looming and Satan demanding his bride, will Arik and Limos surrender to the desire smoldering between them? Or will giving in to their passion unleash hell on earth?</span>

<div class='questionText'>
<a href="/questions/1130728-i-skimmed-some-of-the-reviews-and-was">I skimmed some of the reviews and was disheartened about the rape scene. Is this ever adressed in a good manner or really handled with scorn for the victim like some readers said?</a>
</div>

<div class='communityAnswer'>
<div class='communityAnswerBody'>
<div class='answererUserIcon'>
<a class="leftAlignedImage userPhoto" href="/user/show/8850788-wendi"><img alt="" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/users/1534975471i/8850788._UY100_CR26,0,100,100_.jpg" /></a>
</div>
<div class='communityAnswerTextContainer'>
<span class='communityAnswererName'>
<a href="/user/show/8850788-wendi">Wendi</a>
</span>
<span class='communityAnswerText'>
<div class='spoiler'>
This answer contains spoilers…
<span class='spoilerAnswerText'>
<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[
  
    I believe, from my perspective, that she didn't scorn him or even purposefully raped him. She actually threw up after she realized she raped him. At l<a href="#" rel="nofollow noopener">…more</a>
    I believe, from my perspective, that she didn't scorn him or even purposefully raped him. She actually threw up after she realized she raped him. At least, that's how it goes in the audiobook I listened to. I doubt it was re-written. There's more than just rape going on. There was a spell-laced wine involved and Pestilence was behind it. So, no, it wasn't just she tied him down, raped him, and she had no remorse for what she'd done.<a href="#" rel="nofollow noopener">(less)</a>
  
 <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>
</span>
</div>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1141023058" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer528573401145630133"><b>3,5 stars</b><br/><br/>The battle between good and evil continues in Immortal Rider, Larissa Ione’s 2nd book in her Lords of Deliverance Series.<br/><br/>Limo, Horsewoman of the Apocalypse and Arik Wagner, human, working or the US Army’s paranormal unit , are unable to fight the attraction they feel for each when they first meet – something that will have the most devastating repercussions in their lives.<br/><br/>What else can happen in Limos life? Not only is she fighting to keep her Seal from breaking, holding back secrets fr</span>
  <span id="freeText528573401145630133" style="display:none"><b>3,5 stars</b><br><br>The battle between good and evil continues in Immortal Rider, Larissa Ione’s 2nd book in her Lords of Deliverance Series.<br><br>Limo, Horsewoman of the Apocalypse and Arik Wagner, human, working or the US Army’s paranormal unit , are unable to fight the attraction they feel for each when they first meet – something that will have the most devastating repercussions in their lives.<br><br>What else can happen in Limos life? Not only is she fighting to keep her Seal from breaking, holding back secrets from her Horsemen brothers….if that’s not enough…she has Satan on the sideline waiting to make her his bride…see, her mother had sold her to Satan when she was a child…and that evil demon demands she remains a virgin until he takes her…even goes as far as kitting her out with a chastity belt!!! Talk about HORROR!!! <blockquote>
  
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1439150545i/15801486.jpg" alt=" photo 301233_1540388407863_1779535798_811399_2043984225_n_zps3t1k2vqb.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  
</blockquote>Into her life – to tempt her away from her virginal life – comes Arik Wagner!!! Sexy and dangerous seducer!!!!! <blockquote>
  
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1439150545i/15801487.jpg" alt=" photo 8f6b74b01c51f2555e338df8bad8a415_zpsxlccnzav.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  
</blockquote> Okay, the sexual chemistry between these two was hot and sizzling…..so f…..k Satan…..he wanted Limos …she wanted him…and they spend a rather short but fab time in bed!!!!! <blockquote>
  
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1439150545i/15801488.jpg" alt=" photo Sharing-Harper-e1374697076466_zps20c6e633.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  
</blockquote>Yes, that’s right…Satan is going to get Arik’s ass for deflowering his future bride!!! <br><br>That’s exactly what happens. Arik is dragged into Hell where he’s tortured for a while before he’s rescued by one of his demon friends.<br><br>I adored these two characters. They were really cute , trying to find a way to be together ….and I simply loved the playful banter with each other….<blockquote>
  
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1439150545i/15801489.jpg" alt=" photo cfeaea8d13fb95ae450fb4ebfad464a8_zpsgu9trw9b.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  
</blockquote> Doomsday is looming….fierce battles, twists and turns, treachery, new enemies…..it’s a non-stop ride.<br><br>One of the things I enjoy in this series is how the author incorporates characters from the Demonica books into the stories.<br><br>This is a series I can so recommend to lovers of sexy and dark paranormal romance.<br><br><b>My favorite quote:</b><br><blockquote>

<div id="review_296976787" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/296976787" />
    <a title="D.G." class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/210123-d-g"><img alt="D.G." src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1330353755p2/210123.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/296976787?book_show_action=true">Mar 19, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="D.G." class="user" itemprop="url" name="D.G." href="/user/show/210123-d-g">D.G.</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9780446574471" href="/book/show/11350552-immortal-rider">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/210123-d-g?shelf=audiobook">audiobook</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/210123-d-g?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/210123-d-g?shelf=sucked">sucked</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/210123-d-g?shelf=will-not-continue-series">will-not-continue-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/210123-d-g?shelf=wtf">wtf</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer296976787" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17760913057957122027">***RANT BELOW WITH SPOILERS***<br/><br/>This one star rating is not because the main plot but because of a sub plot that led to book #3 in the series. On it's own, this book was OK even if I found the business of unconditional love a bit dubious given what Limos had done..."so you were responsible for the death of my children? Of course I forgive you!!"<br/><br/>My main gripe with this book is that it had one of the most disgusting setups for a couple I've seen. I was so full of rage when I finished reading that I </span>
  <span id="freeText17760913057957122027" style="display:none">***RANT BELOW WITH SPOILERS***<br /><br />This one star rating is not because the main plot but because of a sub plot that led to book #3 in the series. On it's own, this book was OK even if I found the business of unconditional love a bit dubious given what Limos had done..."so you were responsible for the death of my children? Of course I forgive you!!"<br /><br />My main gripe with this book is that it had one of the most disgusting setups for a couple I've seen. I was so full of rage when I finished reading that I couldn't sleep at all. So what happened in this book that disturbed me so? One of the characters was raped AND THE NEXT BOOK HAS THIS PERSON PAIRED UP WITH THE RAPIST. <br /><br />Yup. The rapist and the victim, together for ever and ever.<br /><br />Shocked yet? Well, there's a twist that makes it OK in the eyes of Ms. Ione. Because in this case, the WOMAN RAPED THE GUY.<br /><br />How could this be, you may wonder? It's very simple.<br />- She drugged him.<br />- She restrained him.<br />- She rode him like a pony while the guy said no over and over and over.<br /><br />I was so disgusted by this scene that I doubt I'll read any book by Ms. Ione again.<br /><br />Worse, NOBODY in the freaking book came to the guy's defense. Several characters had the GALL to say that he got laid, what's the problem? Like a man doesn't have the right to decide where he puts his penis or whether or not he wants to father a child with a particular woman.<br /><br />Oh yes, that's the cherry on top. The goal of this rape was to get the man to father a child to "save the world". Yes, these people, who ARE SUPPOSEDLY the good guys, created a baby, without the consent of his father, to use him for who knows what purposes and then throw him aside when they're done with him to be reared by SOMEBODY ELSE. Yes, the rapist is not even going to keep the child or even tell the father, hey you, I had a baby when I raped you, do you want it?<br /><br />But you may say...that's not the way it was! There were some attenuating circumstances! She did it to save the world! She didn't know the wine was drugged! She didn't know she had restrained him! She didn't realize he meant it when he said no! But those are excuses. First, if the goal was to save the world, why didn't they ask him? Why did they have to go against his back? (The scroll didn't say the baby had to be conceived in secret.) Second, she knew the wine had some magic and she didn't know what kind, that's why she didn't want to drink it in the first place. Third, she knew that her ability came out during sex and that's why she wasn't having any. But the most important thing is that the man told her repeatedly NO OVER AND OVER. That should have been enough for her to stop.<br /><br />Women have been dealing with double standards for a long time and if we want to get rid of them, we shouldn't do it ourselves. If it's wrong for a man to take a woman without her consent, then it's wrong for a woman to do the same. Or do we think that equality means that now we have the right to trample and violate men? <br /><br />Obviously, I won't be reading the next book in the series. I never got the point of fan fiction, but I'm tempted to write one myself where the rapist gets what she deserves.</span>
  <a data-text-id="17760913057957122027" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer14499938494868920181">Totally enjoyed this tale of Limos, the only female rider of the four horsemen of the apocalypse, and how she came to fall in love with Erik of the Aegis. Limos has the unfortunate circumstance of being betrothed to Satan (poor girl) and any time a man gets close to her, there are bad consequences. So when Erik tries to kiss her one night at a party, he is dragged down into the underworld and tortured. <br/><br/>A good chunk of the book focuses on PTSD and Erik’s recovery, which was interesting, and also </span>
  <span id="freeText14499938494868920181" style="display:none">Totally enjoyed this tale of Limos, the only female rider of the four horsemen of the apocalypse, and how she came to fall in love with Erik of the Aegis. Limos has the unfortunate circumstance of being betrothed to Satan (poor girl) and any time a man gets close to her, there are bad consequences. So when Erik tries to kiss her one night at a party, he is dragged down into the underworld and tortured. <br /><br />A good chunk of the book focuses on PTSD and Erik’s recovery, which was interesting, and also Limos had to right a lot of the wrongs she had made in the past. This book also featured the set up for two characters I assume will feature in the next book, another of the horsemen (Death) Thanedos, who reminds me a lot of Zsadist from the BDB, both in manner and appearance, and Reagan, also from the Aegis. They promise to be a spicy couple, and the way their story was set up to start in the next book really ends on a cliffhanger! <br /><br />Please excuse typos/name misspellings. Entered on screen reader.<br /></span>

<div id="review_1405572566" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1405572566" />
    <a title="Sophia Triad" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/44642860-sophia-triad"><img alt="Sophia Triad" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1591419108p2/44642860.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1405572566?book_show_action=true">Oct 01, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sophia Triad" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sophia Triad" href="/user/show/44642860-sophia-triad">Sophia Triad</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=worldend-endofworldasweknowit">worldend-endofworldasweknowit</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=1paranormal-lovestories">1paranormal-lovestories</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=afterlife">afterlife</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=angels">angels</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=immortals">immortals</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=demons">demons</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1405572566" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15778589598783318204"><b>
  <i>"Hellooooo. I'm a Horseman of the Apocalypse, and I'm betrothed to the most infamous, most powerful demon in existence. I couldn't draw more attention to myself if I wore Lady Gaga's meat dress to a PETA convention.”</i>
</b><br/><br/>After Sin, we encounter another unlucky girl in the series. Limos may be one of the horsemen, all powerful and mighty and mistress of Famine, but she is unfortunately also Satan’s future bride. <br/>This could be another example of a forced marriage; however Limos will not yield that </span>
  <span id="freeText15778589598783318204" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>"Hellooooo. I'm a Horseman of the Apocalypse, and I'm betrothed to the most infamous, most powerful demon in existence. I couldn't draw more attention to myself if I wore Lady Gaga's meat dress to a PETA convention.”</i>
</b><br /><br />After Sin, we encounter another unlucky girl in the series. Limos may be one of the horsemen, all powerful and mighty and mistress of Famine, but she is unfortunately also Satan’s future bride. <br />This could be another example of a forced marriage; however Limos will not yield that easily. Obviously Satan can be very persuasive and very jealous of his future wife.<br /><br />Arik Wagner really likes Limos (Arik is brother of Runa and consequently Shade’s brother in law). Limos is trying to keep her distance, mainly for his own good. Sadly, Arik does not know his place and a stolen kiss will land him in Hell. The place where jealous fiancé Satan rules. The place where Arik will be tortured continually until he loses his mind.<br /><br />The book is the story of Arik and Limos’ sexy games, Arik’s survival, Satan’s revenge and of course the prevention of Apocalypses. Limos has to keep her seal safe and Reseph/Pestilence has to be stopped. Since Arik is Runa’s brother, this is also a family matter for the Seminus demons brothers.<br /><br />Pestilence is such a bad boy. His book with his HEA will come later on; nevertheless he is the character you love to hate.<br /><br />Regan and Thanatos’ story is stealing the show in the end and the next book about Thanatos will definitely be an emotional rollercoaster. A road set on deception and betrayal.<br /><br />I absolutely loved this book. I devoured each page. I was making guesses which secondary character deserves his/her own book (hint: Reaver and Harvester clearly).<br />I got lost in this magical world, where even Hell apparently is livable.</span>
  <a data-text-id="15778589598783318204" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_237170981" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/237170981" />
    <a title="Kat Kennedy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3270188-kat-kennedy"><img alt="Kat Kennedy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1537750381p2/3270188.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/237170981?book_show_action=true">Nov 18, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kat Kennedy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kat Kennedy" href="/user/show/3270188-kat-kennedy">Kat Kennedy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3270188-kat-kennedy?shelf=romance-romance-romance">romance-romance-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3270188-kat-kennedy?shelf=kat-s-book-reviews">kat-s-book-reviews</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer237170981" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6205424867347333898">I still remember the first time I rode a horse which is synonymous as saying I still remember the time I almost died. That hellbeast ran riot across a large desert area surrounding a partially active volcano and laughed at my feeble attempts to summon help or stop his rampage.<br/><br/>What this earned for me was a year or two of riding lessons because where I grew up, riding lessons were the thing to do for proper young ladies. As there is nothing proper about me, you can be sure that I never progressed </span>
  <span id="freeText6205424867347333898" style="display:none">I still remember the first time I rode a horse which is synonymous as saying I still remember the time I almost died. That hellbeast ran riot across a large desert area surrounding a partially active volcano and laughed at my feeble attempts to summon help or stop his rampage.<br /><br />What this earned for me was a year or two of riding lessons because where I grew up, riding lessons were the thing to do for proper young ladies. As there is nothing proper about me, you can be sure that I never progressed much past being able to keep my seat and to pick a good horse that would stop when I politely asked it to. A surprising amount of horse riding comes down to just picking the right horse. Some horses are always bad because they hate you and secretly long to tear into your entrails despite masquerading as a herbivore. Other horses are flighty and will have their good or bad moments. So for the most part, you pick a good horse and stick with it. <br /> <br />Authors tend to be like a horse. You find a good one and stick with it and they usually won’t fail you. This analogy is especially true for the Paranormal Romance genre where books tend to be serialized. I’ve tried to ride a series that was flighty with books wavering between good and bad like a toddler on too much sugar. It’s a frustrating experience.<br /><br />If I had to pick my favourite horse though, Larrisa Ione would be it. I don’t know how she would feel to being referred to as a horse, but there it is. I’ve generally found her work to be consistently readable.<br /><br />Immortal Rider is the story of a Horseman of the Apocalypse and a human man falling in love and dealing with her lying and evil brothers and the fact that she had him dragged into hell for kissing her. Completely normal stuff that I’m sure we can all relate to. <br /> <br />I have some issues with female representation in her novels and particularly this one. However, over all, I do enjoy her storytelling and her characters. <br /><br />Her novels also tend to have the appropriate amount of cheesy goodness in them without overdoing it or crossing into the realm of dumbassery. Something that’s surprisingly easy to do in this genre.<br />I think, if I’d read the first novel, I would have enjoyed this more as opposed to playing catch up and trying to familiarize myself with a world that seems to take it for granted that you already know most of the characters.<br /><br />Ione’s novels are, at least in my opinion, better than the usual fare and they have a great deal of imagination and interesting world building in them. So if you’ve lost your seat in this genre and are looking for a good horse, maybe give Ione a chance. <br /> <br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="6205424867347333898" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/159414762?book_show_action=true">Apr 07, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Anzu The Great Destroyer" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Anzu The Great Destroyer" href="/user/show/2278800-anzu-the-great-destroyer">Anzu The Great Destroyer</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/11015247-immortal-rider">review of another edition</a>

          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">fans of the author</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2278800-anzu-the-great-destroyer?shelf=fanged-and-deadly">fanged-and-deadly</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2278800-anzu-the-great-destroyer?shelf=is-it-just-me-goddammit">is-it-just-me-goddammit</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2278800-anzu-the-great-destroyer?shelf=cheesetacular">cheesetacular</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer159414762" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12656940806269162057">I’ve been waiting for months for <i>Immortal Rider</i>. I kept on stalking Larissa Ione’s blog, me being such a big fan and all, watching her news, avoiding spoilers and so on. Finally I managed to get the book and the time to read it.<br/> <br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380348041ra/702359.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>The question of the day would be: <b>Am I happy with this book? Was it everything I was hoping for? Did I do the happy dance after finishing it?</b><br/><br/>No.<br/><br/>*review ends here*<br/><br/>.<br/><br/>.<br/><br/>.<br/><br/>Nah, hold your horses people, of course I’m not done with <s>f*cking up</s> reviewing the book. Of course I have </span>
  <span id="freeText12656940806269162057" style="display:none">I’ve been waiting for months for <i>Immortal Rider</i>. I kept on stalking Larissa Ione’s blog, me being such a big fan and all, watching her news, avoiding spoilers and so on. Finally I managed to get the book and the time to read it.<br> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380348041ra/702359.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The question of the day would be: <b>Am I happy with this book? Was it everything I was hoping for? Did I do the happy dance after finishing it?</b><br><br>No.<br><br>*review ends here*<br><br>.<br><br>.<br><br>.<br><br>Nah, hold your horses people, of course I’m not done with <s>f*cking up</s> reviewing the book. Of course I have to ramble about it for at least 15 minutes. That’s the way I work.<br><br>What is my problem you ask? First of all the story sucks balls. Yes, balls. Listen to this:<br><br>We have a little horseperson, Limos. She’s a badass warrior who dresses like a Hawaian reject and always smells like coconut. I presume so far that even her sweat smells like coconut. I didn’t want to get into intimate details with this so let’s just stop with sweat. Ok so she meets the hot dude Arik. He’s a human of course. You will never have two badass warriors hooking up; things would be too easy then. No fun in things being too easy. So after they kiss the dude ends up in Hell and gets tortured for a month. He escapes and forgives the chick just because she’s hot. Bla bla bla flirting oral sex bla bla bla. Then we find out that (I’ll put this in bold because it’s priceless) <b> she is wearing a chastity belt and only her husband can remove it</b>. The funny thing is that this is not the best part of it. Hold on, I’m getting to it. So apart from the chastity belt<br> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380348041ra/702360.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>we have the following: <b> she is betrothed to Satan</b> (yes, freakin’ Satan) <b>and he wants her fresh and untouched</b>. You guessed it right. UNTOUCHED. AKA a virgin. So she needs someone to take away her maidenhood and save her from being raped by Satan.<br> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380348041ra/702361.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Ok so after you’ve read this what’s your opinion on <i>Immortal Rider</i>? I don’t know if I should laugh or cry. I mean this is a joke! I can’t process it… *facepalm*<br><br>Second (remember the first - up there somewhere), the characters suck. Limos is not my favorite horseman and Arik is just… meh. Nothing special about him, don’t like him don’t hate him. He just exists. Period. <br><br>So sucky story and meh characters = bad book and me punching a kid in the face. See what you made me do Mrs. Ione? See what you made me do??<br><br>*clears throat*<br><br>So yeah, saying that I’m having issues with this book is an understatement.<br><br>There’s actually something I liked about <i>Immortal Rider</i> and if I’m not wrong I said this about <i>Eternal Rider</i> as well. I loved Wraith, Thanatos and (surprisingly) Regan. They’re the main reason for me not giving it two stars.<br><br>So the conclusion? I’m totally neutral about this. I won’t say I hate it because I still like Larissa Ione but it’s the last chance I’m giving her. One more <s>mistake</s> book like this and I’m blowing everything up!</span>
  <a data-text-id="12656940806269162057" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22911953-monty-cupcake-queen-of-bloodshed?shelf=2017">2017</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22911953-monty-cupcake-queen-of-bloodshed?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2071278426" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13248687528497147485">Barely 3 stars. It took me a couple days to finish this because I got bored. I stopped reading and had to force myself to pick this book back up and finish it. <br/><br/>I wasn't looking forward to this book anyway because neither of the main characters interested me. Limos came off bratty and flippant in the other books. Arik seemed super human and military. Limos stayed the same, but Arik improved. <br/><br/>The plot: Arik kisses Limos and is dragged to hell to be tortured because Limos is engaged to Satan and no</span>
  <span id="freeText13248687528497147485" style="display:none">Barely 3 stars. It took me a couple days to finish this because I got bored. I stopped reading and had to force myself to pick this book back up and finish it. <br /><br />I wasn't looking forward to this book anyway because neither of the main characters interested me. Limos came off bratty and flippant in the other books. Arik seemed super human and military. Limos stayed the same, but Arik improved. <br /><br />The plot: Arik kisses Limos and is dragged to hell to be tortured because Limos is engaged to Satan and no one touches his fiancée. Arik gets out of hell and the romance is on. <br /><br />Arik really grew as a character and I enjoyed the times the book was from his POV. He changes from super soldier all up in the military to helping the horsemen and working for good in different ways. He's a very adaptable character. <br /><br />Limos stayed the same, that of a bratty teenager whose main activity is lying and blowing off things. That's all Limos does, party and lie. I didn't like her or care for her and her lying was the main plot after Arik was out of hell. She was too juvenile. <br /><br />The romance was sweet and PG-13 as Limos has some restrictions on her activities. It was also a teen feeling romance due to Limos' lack of maturity. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="13248687528497147485" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

    <a title="Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog"><img alt="Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1352609417p2/2489554.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/142618215?book_show_action=true">Jan 21, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)" href="/user/show/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog">Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Paranormal Romance fans, Demonica fans</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=pnr">pnr</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=warriors">warriors</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=review-requests">review-requests</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=books-i-own">books-i-own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=read-in-2011">read-in-2011</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=author-larissa-ione">author-larissa-ione</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer142618215" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4769197395573294609">I have been eagerly anticipating Arik Wagner’s book for a long time. I adored him in the Demonica series and now, with his own book, the hot human brother finally gets his chance to shine. So going into this book, I was already giddy because I would get some Arik action.<br/><br/>Enter Limos aka Famine, the only female horseman. Before she was even born, she was promised to the Dark Lord. Being unwillingly betrothed to Satan brings up a lot of problems. But when Arik can’t deny his attraction to Limos any</span>
  <span id="freeText4769197395573294609" style="display:none">I have been eagerly anticipating Arik Wagner’s book for a long time. I adored him in the Demonica series and now, with his own book, the hot human brother finally gets his chance to shine. So going into this book, I was already giddy because I would get some Arik action.<br /><br />Enter Limos aka Famine, the only female horseman. Before she was even born, she was promised to the Dark Lord. Being unwillingly betrothed to Satan brings up a lot of problems. But when Arik can’t deny his attraction to Limos any longer, he kisses her. And this is when the story begins its hellride. And I mean, literally.<br /><br />Just as Arik gets summoned to hell, Limos tells him to never, ever speak her name. If he does while in agony, then Limos will find herself next to her rightful husband. <br /><br />Larissa Ione had created a unique and darkly sensual world in the Lord of Deliverance series. I loved the entire concept. She isn’t afraid to put her characters through tough experiences in order to tell their story right and I have to respect that. <br /><br />Arik and Limos endure a lot of things that would normally break a person. So it was interesting to read about their journey through that as well as see the development of their romance together. Though I did like the romance between Li and Arik, I didn’t think it was one of Ione’s best. Her Demonica series still stands as number one for me. However, I have a feeling that the next book, Lethal Rider will be the hitter for me. <br /><br />Than and Regan’s chemistry was palpable and I really enjoyed their parts of the books. It makes my hands itch for the next one and I’m sensing that Ione will surely deliver another one of her epic stories for the sassy Aegis chick and Death.<br /><br />On the flip side, there were two things that didn’t exactly thrill me about this book. The first is that I hated the secrets between Limos and Arik. This may be just a personal preference, but I don’t usually enjoy stories where there is a communication problem between the hero and heroine. Most of the time I feel like it can be easily solved. However, that is not to say that it was a bad conflict. It was just okay.<br /><br />The other thing is that Limos got a little annoying in some areas. Not all, but enough that she got some eye rolls. Again, nothing too over the top, but I still had to consider that when rating this book. Ergooooooo, 4 stars! <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="4769197395573294609" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_231068227" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/231068227" />
    <a title="Jen Davis" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4669344-jen-davis"><img alt="Jen Davis" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1548427639p2/4669344.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/231068227?book_show_action=true">Nov 04, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jen Davis" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jen Davis" href="/user/show/4669344-jen-davis">Jen Davis</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4669344-jen-davis?shelf=arcs">arcs</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4669344-jen-davis?shelf=pararnormal-romance">pararnormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4669344-jen-davis?shelf=demonica">demonica</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer231068227" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8222083349253705689">One of the things I like best about Larissa Ione is that her books are unpredictable. And there is always so much going on. And they are so freaking hot! (I guess that's more than one thing, but let me gush for a moment.) I enjoyed <i>Eternal Rider</i>, but it took me a little while to get into. Not the case here. This story reeled me in from the beginning and didn't let go.<br/><br/>Limos is the only female among the Horsemen of the Apocalypse. She is as beautiful as she is deadly. She is also a virgin. Limos w</span>
  <span id="freeText8222083349253705689" style="display:none">One of the things I like best about Larissa Ione is that her books are unpredictable. And there is always so much going on. And they are so freaking hot! (I guess that's more than one thing, but let me gush for a moment.) I enjoyed <i>Eternal Rider</i>, but it took me a little while to get into. Not the case here. This story reeled me in from the beginning and didn't let go.<br /><br />Limos is the only female among the Horsemen of the Apocalypse. She is as beautiful as she is deadly. She is also a virgin. Limos was promised to Satan as his bride when she born. She wears a chastity belt that attacks anyone who tries to get in her pants. And if she ever allows herself to give in to an attraction to another man, it's bad news for the object of her affection.<br /><br />Arik's been part of the Demonica world for a long time. He is Runa's brother and part of the military force that fights deadly supernaturals. He is drawn to Limos, and as the book begins, he finally gives in to the temptation to kiss her. That's when everything goes to hell. Literally. Satan's minions set out to torture him... the curse saying that if he screams Limos' name in agony, she'll have to return to the Underworld and take her place at Satan's side.<br /><br />This is only the beginning of a long journey for these two. Of course, Arik makes it out, but one obstacle after another is thrown in their path. Not the least of which is Limos' own shady past and the looming damage it could do if it comes to light. Pestilence has a hand in all the madness. And there is a great side story featuring the angels Reaver and Harvester.<br /><br />Oh! And speaking of great side stories... I loved, loved, loved the direction Ione is taking with Thanatos. I feared his story was going to be predictable with the nature of his seal, but I was dead wrong. The great b-plot stuff just wasn't there in the last book, but it definitely is here --and it's a big win.<br /><br />I will acknowledge: it takes forever for sexual payoff between our main characters. But there is plenty of sexy action going on throughout the book. I won't spoil the details, but... wow. The whole thing was really good. And I. Am. Dying. For the next book. Almost 5 stars.<br /><br /><br /><i>*ARC Provided by Grand Central Publishing</i></span>

          </span>

<div id="review_241360041" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/241360041" />
    <a title="Melindeeloo" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2766907-melindeeloo"><img alt="Melindeeloo" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1266031818p2/2766907.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/241360041?book_show_action=true">Nov 29, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Melindeeloo" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Melindeeloo" href="/user/show/2766907-melindeeloo">Melindeeloo</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9780446574471" href="/book/show/11350552-immortal-rider">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2766907-melindeeloo?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2766907-melindeeloo?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2766907-melindeeloo?shelf=demons">demons</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer241360041" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17993107649386786869">No blurb this time 'round. I started Immortal Rider the day it came out and read the first hundred pages and put the book down. This Demonica spinoff and the Demonica books themselves have always had some darkness to them but this first part of book was filled with torture of the hero, violation of a continuing character, and more of Pestilence's depravity just tossed off in the background - I just got tired of being bludgeoned with how evil the bad guys were and set the book aside. <br/><br/>I did end up</span>
  <span id="freeText17993107649386786869" style="display:none">No blurb this time 'round. I started Immortal Rider the day it came out and read the first hundred pages and put the book down. This Demonica spinoff and the Demonica books themselves have always had some darkness to them but this first part of book was filled with torture of the hero, violation of a continuing character, and more of Pestilence's depravity just tossed off in the background - I just got tired of being bludgeoned with how evil the bad guys were and set the book aside. <br /><br />I did end up picking this back up, but I struggled through to the 2/3rds mark where the action finally kicked in. I think that the reason that this was such a difficult read for me is that I just never got to the point where I clicked with Limos, actually I didn't much like her and never came to care about her redemption. Normally, a great hero can offset a less than stellar heroine but Arik, despite his interesting history and secret powers, was pretty generic for a leading man. It didn't help that the romance between them didn't work for me either, how does one get past all the deception and torture – not as easy breezy as it is done here for sure.<br /><br />One of the things that kept me reading to the bitter end was that I really liked Thanatos and his thread had a better build up than Limos/Arik's right up to the 'completion' of Regan's mission which was shockingly terrible. In fact all of the 'deflowerings' in Immortal Rider were squicky. So the lack of the normally uber steamy build up to a satisfying consummation - times two - dropped the book from marginally okay to not. <br /><br />So bottom line, I am not exactly sure what to say. I guess that Immortal Rider felt more UF-y and less romance-y to me (or perhaps a horror romance), the focus is not as much on the relationship as the events and plotting to put the elements of the Apocalypse in play. And as to future books – I am still sort of interested in Thanatos' book but I absolutely agree with whoever said way back when that they didn't want to see a story for a redeemed Harvester with a salvaged Reseph as a book four. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="17993107649386786869" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_459127080" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/459127080" />
    <a title="Sammy Loves Books" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14227114-sammy-loves-books"><img alt="Sammy Loves Books" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1534119573p2/14227114.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/459127080?book_show_action=true">Nov 19, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sammy Loves Books" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sammy Loves Books" href="/user/show/14227114-sammy-loves-books">Sammy Loves Books</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14227114-sammy-loves-books?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14227114-sammy-loves-books?shelf=angels-are-sexy">angels-are-sexy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14227114-sammy-loves-books?shelf=violence-torture-gore">violence-torture-gore</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14227114-sammy-loves-books?shelf=demons-rock">demons-rock</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14227114-sammy-loves-books?shelf=virgins-like-sex-too">virgins-like-sex-too</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14227114-sammy-loves-books?shelf=forced-seduction">forced-seduction</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer459127080" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4607322667468845150">It's hard to enjoy a love story when you don't like the heroine or the hero. I rated this book a 2 because I outright disliked Limos and there was nothing special about Arik. This book would have been a solid 4 star if I could have cared if the main couple found love. Limos lies so much to everyone around her: her brothers, and Arik, the man she claims to love. She even kills Sartel to protect her lies because he was about to spill the beans. Arik made for a boring hero that I never connected wi</span>
  <span id="freeText4607322667468845150" style="display:none">It's hard to enjoy a love story when you don't like the heroine or the hero. I rated this book a 2 because I outright disliked Limos and there was nothing special about Arik. This book would have been a solid 4 star if I could have cared if the main couple found love. Limos lies so much to everyone around her: her brothers, and Arik, the man she claims to love. She even kills Sartel to protect her lies because he was about to spill the beans. Arik made for a boring hero that I never connected with. So what if he made it thru a month of torture without turning on Limos. I have read torture scenes that make me feel for the hero, ie (the Dark Hunter, Acheron and BDB's Zadist). The writing was so bland however that I felt nothing for Arik and the pain he was experiencing.<br /><br />For the 1st time in a long time I actually stopped reading this book because there was so much violence that I didn't care about. It was overkill and became redundant.<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ The love story that begins to develop between Regan and Than became the best part of the book and overshadowed the main characters. That was until Regan drugged and raped Than and took his virginity against his will.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> This book almost became a "Did Not Finish" at that point, but I had to know how it all ended. What really bothers me is, how can Regan ever redeem herself enough for me to want to read their love story. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ I could never accept a love story if a hero had raped his female, but she were to forgive him and fall in love with him. So how am I suppose to accept that Than can let go of the rage and humiliation he feels after being violated, and that he will fall for his rapist. Worst, Than had so much rage after he was violated that he sent out a death wave killing thousands so his brother and sister paralyzed him with Hellhound saliva. Just more torture for one of my favorite characters. Uhg!! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />I enjoyed Ares book and couldn't wait to read about Limos and Arik, but this book was a major let down. I am not even interested in reading about Regan and Than. </span>
  <a data-text-id="4607322667468845150" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="♡Karlyn P♡" class="user" itemprop="url" name="♡Karlyn P♡" href="/user/show/1131400-karlyn-p">♡Karlyn P♡</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1131400-karlyn-p?shelf=genre-paranromal">genre-paranromal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1131400-karlyn-p?shelf=published-2011">published-2011</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1131400-karlyn-p?shelf=read-2012">read-2012</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer194597849" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6713782619555894935">And the plot thickens! Whew, I loved it and now I can't wait for the next. <br/><br/>In this second book, Limos is faced with her many past lies as they come back to haunt her. Long ago she made a deal with the devil, literally, and now those she has come to care about are going to learn of her lies unless she can stop those who threaten to reveal her secrets. <br/><br/>Arik is the human who has been lusting after Limos, and after one quick kiss he finds himself fighting for his life as demons try to torture and pu</span>
  <span id="freeText6713782619555894935" style="display:none">And the plot thickens! Whew, I loved it and now I can't wait for the next. <br /><br />In this second book, Limos is faced with her many past lies as they come back to haunt her. Long ago she made a deal with the devil, literally, and now those she has come to care about are going to learn of her lies unless she can stop those who threaten to reveal her secrets. <br /><br />Arik is the human who has been lusting after Limos, and after one quick kiss he finds himself fighting for his life as demons try to torture and punish him. Limos is the intended bride of Satan, and she even wears his chastity belt, so no man can have her. <br /><br />Limos helps rescue Arik, and they find themselves working together to find her agimortus (sp?), one of four tokens that can help stop the apocalypse. They must also battle Reseph/Pestilence as he tries to find ways to break the seals that protect the remaining horsemen from turning evil. I enjoyed how Arik got Limos to slowly respect the power of truth instead relying on lying, and how her love for Arik became more powerful to her than evil. They made a great pair. <br /><br />The other romance brewing is with Than, who is forced to accommodate the sexy Regan while she does research on the horsemen to help figure out how to stop the apocalypse. However, she has nefarious intentions which has Than blowing his f'n mind in fury. (Oh, I can't wait for their story next!!)<br /><br />This is the most intense PNR series I've ever read, built around a richly detailed paranormal world of vampires, demons, humans, angels and much more. It's a spinoff from her Demonica series, but with more complexities and greater evils. I'll admit it's a challenge to follow as there are so many characters with so many magical gifts, but well worth it. I am in total awe of Larissa Ione for being able to weave such complex world and keep all these characters straight. Amazing! <br /><br /><br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="6713782619555894935" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/238758756?book_show_action=true">Nov 22, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="willaful" class="user" itemprop="url" name="willaful" href="/user/show/2833071-willaful">willaful</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9781455504855" href="/book/show/11601650-immortal-rider">review of another edition</a>

          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">people who've read the first book</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2833071-willaful?shelf=made-me-laugh">made-me-laugh</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2833071-willaful?shelf=not-a-stand-alone">not-a-stand-alone</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2833071-willaful?shelf=heroines-behaving-badly">heroines-behaving-badly</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2833071-willaful?shelf=tortured-hero">tortured-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2833071-willaful?shelf=ick-factor">ick-factor</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2833071-willaful?shelf=special-needs-addiction">special-needs-addiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2833071-willaful?shelf=man-bites-dog">man-bites-dog</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer238758756" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9679831048858156303">The Lords of Deliverance series gets even more complex and addictive in the second book. Although there’s still a primary romance, there’s a whole lot more going on, as those characters on the side of Evil work to bring about the Apocalypse and those on the side of Good work to prevent it.<br/><br/>Limos aka Famine, the sole female horseman of the Apocalypse, has two big problems: she’s betrothed to Satan, and she has some very ugly secrets she’s keeping from her brothers. When a human male named Arik kis</span>
  <span id="freeText9679831048858156303" style="display:none">The Lords of Deliverance series gets even more complex and addictive in the second book. Although there’s still a primary romance, there’s a whole lot more going on, as those characters on the side of Evil work to bring about the Apocalypse and those on the side of Good work to prevent it.<br /><br />Limos aka Famine, the sole female horseman of the Apocalypse, has two big problems: she’s betrothed to Satan, and she has some very ugly secrets she’s keeping from her brothers. When a human male named Arik kisses her, it arouses Satan’s jealousy and Arik winds up tortured in hell, an event that helps cement the feelings growing between him and Limos. Meanwhile, the turned-evil horseman Pestilence is growing ever stronger -- and he happens to be the only other person who knows Limos’s secrets. And the evil-fighting Aegis have hatched a plan to seduce Limos’s brother Thanatos (Death) in a way that could prove ultimately disastrous.<br /><br />As you might expect from a book about the battle between good and evil, some of the characters here spend a lot of time being, well, evil. Which makes for some very painful reading at times, as both major and minor characters are frequently tortured and injured. Even knowing that most can be healed or regenerated, it makes for a rough ride at times. Thankfully, there’s also the romance, steamy scenes, and some humor to relieve the tension; I especially enjoyed how Arik, refusing to say Limos’s name, takes to calling her “Flicka” and “Secretariat.”<br /><br />This is a series that really needs to be read as a set, and preferably after reading the “Demonica” series. Although there’s enough resolution to make the ending bearable for romance readers, there’s obviously plenty more story to come.<br /><br />(reviewed from e-arc provided by netGalley)</span>
  <a data-text-id="9679831048858156303" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

Mainly, it was to shut her up, but he also wanted to prove her wrong, show her that for all her protests, she’d wanted that kiss outside Ares’s mansion. She might be a Biblical legend, and he a mere human, but when their bodies touched, they were man and woman, and neither had any tactical advantage. Her entire body went taut, but then her tongue met his, and it was game over. He’d won. He’d made his point.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>UPDATE ver.3, May, 23rd </b><br />Again, Larissa Ione posted new snippet (Does she know all of this snippet will killin me? A sexy, gorgeous lunatic in a hot pink bikini. With a white flower in her hair. No one looking at her would know that the ultra-feminine woman doing the hula could kick ass like the newest-model Terminator.<br /><br />Arik laid out the towel and sank down in the sand, back against a palm tree, his fingers gripping a cold beer so tight he figured it was close to shatter threshold. How could she dance like that without spilling her margarita?<br /><br />When she spotted him, she stilled, her too-gorgeous-to-be-real eyes drilling into him. In a slow, deliberate motion, she brought her margarita glass to her lips. Her tongue came out and swiped the rim, licking off a line of salt before she locked her lips onto the glass and sipped. In Arik’s hand, the beer bottle shook.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />Just wanna say :<br /><b> DECEMBER PLEASE MOVE FAST!! </b></span>

<div id="review_138049992" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/138049992" />
    <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie"><img alt="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514769932p2/3275325.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/138049992?book_show_action=true">Jan 02, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie">Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/11015247-immortal-rider">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=read-in-2011">read-in-2011</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer138049992" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17635008092798758456"><i>Immortal Rider</i> is Limos and Arik's story. Limos, aka Famine, is the third horseman (woman) of the Apocalypse. Arik is human and Rune's (from Demonica and Shade's wife) brother and works with human forces to stop the Apocalypse.<br/><br/>This book has so much going on that I don't even know where to start! It immediately begins with Arik kissing Limos and getting taken to Sheoul to be tortured into saying Limos' name. Limos has been betrothed to Satan and no one is allowed intimate relations with her. So, </span>
  <span id="freeText17635008092798758456" style="display:none"><i>Immortal Rider</i> is Limos and Arik's story. Limos, aka Famine, is the third horseman (woman) of the Apocalypse. Arik is human and Rune's (from Demonica and Shade's wife) brother and works with human forces to stop the Apocalypse.<br /><br />This book has so much going on that I don't even know where to start! It immediately begins with Arik kissing Limos and getting taken to Sheoul to be tortured into saying Limos' name. Limos has been betrothed to Satan and no one is allowed intimate relations with her. So, the one thing that didn't measure up is how could Arik, a 'mere' human, withstand all that torture even with being healed?? But he does and he even manages to escape. Of course, Reseph/Pestilence has a big hand in {{all}} things. I do have to say that I liked Arik even more than I had in the Demonica books. He has a lot of gumption for a 'mere' human and I loved how he protected Limos. <br /><br />Speaking of Limos, I'm not too sure how I feel about her. She really comes across as the spoiled baby sister. You do get to know a lot of her history and why she did what she did but she really has to grow and own up to her past. I think she got off easy. I did love the chastity belt though. (LOL) <br /><br />I really enjoyed all the other characters that had decent parts in the book. Of course we have Ares and Cara, who are still great and I loved Cara's ongoing relationships with the animals. I loved the dynamics of all the horsemen with each other and the little tidbits thrown in like how Reseph made them celebrate Christmas. We get a bit of Shade and Runa and a good part with my favorite Seminus demon, Wraith. Reaver and Harvester were quite interesting and I'm not sure how I feel about where that might be going but that seems to be the theme for a few of the possible relationships.<br /><br />So....Reseph/Pestilence, I have no clue how LI will ever EVER redeem him!! I do have to say that he has grabbed my attention from the start and I love all the sweet parts like about Christmas but the orgy part at the end?? uuugghhh that was just nasty! <br /><br />That brings me to Thanatos and Regan. <b>Holy Cow</b>...did that really happen?? I was so sucked into <i>their</i> story that I could care less about Arik/Limos...I just wanted more Thanatos!! I can hardly wait for his book and I can honestly say I have no idea how their relationship can ever recover! Can June please get here faster!!<br /><br />Favorite lines:<br /><br />She'd never wanted to do that to any male. Women who claimed to like it had to be lying. <br /><br />and...<br /><br />"<i>Now</i>, Horsewoman." <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="17635008092798758456" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_153679320" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/153679320" />
    <a title="Amy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3125133-amy"><img alt="Amy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1264894304p2/3125133.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/153679320?book_show_action=true">Mar 11, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Amy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Amy" href="/user/show/3125133-amy">Amy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9780446574471" href="/book/show/11350552-immortal-rider">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3125133-amy?shelf=2readseries">2readseries</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3125133-amy?shelf=fv-review">fv-review</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3125133-amy?shelf=ng-arc">ng-arc</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer153679320" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6006581636649226434"><br/><i>“You,” he purred , “are a HILF.” “A what?” “Horseman I’d like to fuck.”</i><br/><br/>Lethal, sexy Limos is the only female among the four Horseman of the Apocalypse. A virgin who was promised by her mother to Satan as a child, she is bound, literally, by a chastity belt placed on her body by the devil himself until he takes her as his bride. Needless to say, if she ever gives in to her sexual desires or gives her affections to anyImmortal Rider by Larissa Ione male, it will prove deadly. Limos, along with her</span>
  <span id="freeText6006581636649226434" style="display:none"><br /><i>“You,” he purred , “are a HILF.” “A what?” “Horseman I’d like to fuck.”</i><br /><br />Lethal, sexy Limos is the only female among the four Horseman of the Apocalypse. A virgin who was promised by her mother to Satan as a child, she is bound, literally, by a chastity belt placed on her body by the devil himself until he takes her as his bride. Needless to say, if she ever gives in to her sexual desires or gives her affections to anyImmortal Rider by Larissa Ione male, it will prove deadly. Limos, along with her two brothers, are in a continuous battle against their brother, Pestilence (f.k.a. Reseph), who’s seal is broken. Pestilence is the first brother to break his seal, turn evil and now he is on a mission to do the same to his siblings in order to combine evil forces to ignite the Apocalypse.<br /><br />Arik Wagner is a human working for the U.S. Army’s paranormal unit. His job is stressful enough but things get a whole lot messier. Arik attends a celebration at Ares’s mansion after defeating Pestilence’s latest attack. Upon their initial meeting, Arik was immediately attracted to Limos and decided he had nothing to lose by flirting with her at the party. BIG MISTAKE! Arik goes in for a kiss and his day gets shot to hell in a hand basket. The binding contract that Satan has with Limos is such that if any man kisses her, he is sent to Sheoul and tortured until he screams her name in agony. Once her name is uttered, the agreement is set that Limos will willingly take her place as Satan’s bride for eternity. The last words Limos says to Arik before he was taken were “No matter what they do, don’t speak my name!” Arik takes her words to heart and in return he is brutally and continuously tortured and starved. One horrific month later, Arik is rescued from Sheoul and Limos discovers a side of herself she never thought possible. While caring for Arik as he mentally struggles with his return to the real world, she is struck by all that Arik sacrificed on her behalf and realizes she can care for a man other than her brothers. Once Arik is back to his functioning self, he is determined to find a way to break Satan’s contract that looms over Limo’s head.<br /><br />I have to start off in saying that I get giddy when I sit down to open a book by Larissa Ione. After I was introduced to the paranormal world of romance, I tried to get my hands on any and every author that could that could capture a magnificent world and enduring characters like my beloved J.R.Ward. No one could fit the bill until I immersed myself into Ms. Ione’s Demonica series and then my search was over. What adds the “crème de la crème” to her new series are the well-loved Demonica characters who are now a part of the world of The Lords of Deliverance.<br /><br />Eternal Rider sets the stage for The Lords of Deliverance series but Immortal Rider throws you into the no holds barred action of this amazing world. It’s dark, gritty, violent, snarky, sexy and will push boundaries like no other book Ms. Ione has penned. With that said, it is not for the faint of heart or the reader who may have issues with violence and/or torture because Arik faces his share of it and then some. Delivering wicked hot demons and fierce warriors of the Apocalypse, Ms. Ione sets a compelling course to Doomsday as each story unfolds. What you can always count on is even though you are engrossed in an evil and vengeful setting, Ms. Ione’s underlying theme is a desire for the greater good in both mankind and her characters. Limos’ inner nature is to lie but Arik’s kind nature and protectiveness compels her to want to be truthful and an overall better person. She struggles with the secrets and deceptions from her past that have been hidden for too long. Once revealed, Limos expects both her brothers and Arik will never forgive her. Instead, they all are willing to do whatever is necessary to protect Limos and dissolve the contract Satan has condemned her to.<br /><br />Although the book is centered toward Arik and Limos, there are several subplots that continue to set the dark tone of secrets and danger that lurks ahead. Immortal Rider lacked the sexy times I’ve come to expect with Ms. Ione’s main characters, but the sexual tension both Arik and Limos sparked was sizzling and provided affirmation that when they did come together, it was a climactic bombshell of hotness every reader would love! Ms. Ione literally writes some of the most erotic, steamy sex scenes in paranormal romance and the build up to those scenes will have you squirming in your pants! It was an added bonus of humor at how both Limos’ brothers were mortified by the thought of their sister “getting it on” with the “human” and how they struggled not to kick Arik’s ass!<br /><br />Delivering intimidating and captivating characters set against an epic battle of good versus evil, Immortal Rider is nothing short of amazing. Any paranormal reader who has not tapped into the greatness of Larissa Ione needs to start at the beginning with her Demonica series and strap in for an incredible ride.<br /><br /> <br /><br />Favorite Quote: <br /><br /><i>He stepped back from her just enough that he could rake his gaze down her body. “Oh, yeah. I want to take you in every way imaginable and keep you so sexed up that when you aren’t in bed, all you’ll be thinking about is getting back in it.” He took in her lush curves, imagining how well they’d buffer his thrusts. “And that’s just tonight’s itinerary.”</i><br /><br /><br /><br />Originally posted at <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.fictionvixen.com/2011/12/review-immortal-rider-by-larissa-ione.html">http://www.fictionvixen.com/2011/12/r...</a><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="6006581636649226434" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>
